configuration.getBoolean(CommonConfigurationKeys.USE_FIR)\n        )\n    }\n\n    override val pluginId: String get() = COMPILER_PLUGIN_ID\n\n    override val supportsK2: Boolean\n        get() = org.jetbrains.kotlin.utils.addToStdlib.runIf\n\n@OptIn(DirectDeclarationsAccess::class)\nclass FirParcelizeDeclarationGenerator(\n    session: FirSession,\n    private val annotations: List<FqName>\n) : FirDeclarationGenerationExtension(session) {\n    companion object {\n        private val parcelizeMethodsNames = setOf(DESCRIBE_CONTENTS_NAME, WRITE_TO_PARCEL_NAME)\n    }\n\n    private val predicate = DeclarationPredicate.create { annotated(annotations) }\n\n    override fun generateFunctions(callableId: CallableId, context: MemberGenerationContext?): List<FirNamedFunctionSymbol> {\n        val owner = context?.owner as? FirRegularClassSymbol ?: return emptyList()\n        if (!checkParcelizeClassSymbols(owner, session) { session.predicateBasedProvider.matches(predicate, it) }) return emptyList()\n        val function = when (callableId.callableName) {\n            DESCRIBE_CONTENTS_NAME -> {\n                val hasDescribeContentImplementation = owner.hasDescribeContentsImplementation() ||\n                        lookupSuperTypes(owner, lookupInterfaces = false, deep = true, session).any {\n                            it.fullyExpandedType(session).toRegularClassSymbol(session)?.hasDescribeContentsImplementation() ?: false\n                        }\n                runIf(!hasDescribeContentImplementation) {\n                    createMemberFunctionForParcelize(owner, callableId.callableName, session.builtinTypes.intType.coneType)\n                }\n            }\n            WRITE_TO_PARCEL_NAME -> {\n                val declaredFunctions = owner.declarationSymbols.filterIsInstance<FirNamedFunctionSymbol>()\n                runIf(declaredFunctions.none { it.isWriteToParcel() }) {\n                    createMemberFunctionForParcelize(owner, callableId.callableName, session.builtinTypes.unitType.coneType) {\n                        valueParameter(DEST_NAME, PARCEL_ID.createConeType(session))\n                        valueParameter(FLAGS_NAME, session.builtinTypes.intType.coneType)\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            else -> null\n        } ?: return emptyList()\n        return listOf(function.symbol)\n    }\n\n    private fun FirRegularClassSymbol.hasDescribeContentsImplementation(): Boolean {\n        return declarationSymbols.filterIsInstance<FirNamedFunctionSymbol>().any { it.isDescribeContentsImplementation() }\n    }\n\n    private fun FirNamedFunctionSymbol.isDescribeContentsImplementation(): Boolean {\n        if (name != DESCRIBE_CONTENTS_NAME) return false\n        return valueParameterSymbols.isEmpty()\n    }\n\n    private fun FirNamedFunctionSymbol.isWriteToParcel(): Boolean {\n        if (name != WRITE_TO_PARCEL_NAME) return false\n        val parameterSymbols = valueParameterSymbols\n        if (parameterSymbols.size != 2) return false\n        val (destSymbol, flagsSymbol) = parameterSymbols\n        if (destSymbol.resolvedReturnTypeRef.coneType.classId != PARCEL_ID) return false\n        if (!flagsSymbol.resolvedReturnTypeRef.coneType.isInt) return false\n        return true\n    }\n\n    private inline fun createMemberFunctionForParcelize(\n        owner: FirRegularClassSymbol,\n        name: Name,\n        returnType: ConeKotlinType,\n        crossinline init: SimpleFunctionBuildingContext.() -> Unit = {}\n    ): FirNamedFunction {\n        return createMemberFunction(owner, key, name, returnType) {\n            modality = if (owner.modality == Modality.FINAL) Modality.FINAL else Modality.OPEN\n            init()\n        }\n    }\n\n    override fun getCallableNamesForClass(classSymbol: FirClassSymbol<*>, context: MemberGenerationContext): Set<Name> {\n        return when {\n            classSymbol.rawStatus.modality == Modality.ABSTRACT || classSymbol.rawStatus.modality == Modality.SEALED -> emptySet()\n            else -> parcelizeMethodsNames\n        }\n    }\n\n    private val key: GeneratedDeclarationKey\n        get() = ParcelizePluginKey\n\n    override fun FirDeclarationPredicateRegistrar.registerPredicates() ParcelizeSyntheticComponent.ComponentKind,\n            modality: Modality,\n            returnType: KotlinType,\n            vararg parameters: Pair<String, KotlinType>\n        ): SimpleFunctionDescriptor {\n            val functionDescriptor = object : ParcelizeSyntheticComponent, SimpleFunctionDescriptorImpl(\n                classDescriptor,\n                null,\n                Annotations.EMPTY,\n                Name.identifier(componentKind.methodName),\n                CallableMemberDescriptor.Kind.SYNTHESIZED,\n                classDescriptor.source\n            ) {\n                override val componentKind = componentKind\n            }\n\n            val valueParameters = parameters.mapIndexed { index, (name, type) -> functionDescriptor.makeValueParameter(name, type, index) }\n\n            functionDescriptor.initialize(\n                null, classDescriptor.thisAsReceiverParameter, emptyList(), emptyList(), valueParameters,\n                returnType, modality, DescriptorVisibilities.PUBLIC\n            )\n\n            return functionDescriptor\n        }\n\n        private fun    && fromSupertypes.none { it.isDescribeContents() }\n        ) {\n            result += createMethod(thisDescriptor, DESCRIBE_CONTENTS, Modality.OPEN, thisDescriptor.builtIns.intType)\n        } SimpleFunctionDescriptor.isDescribeContents(): Boolean {\n        return this.kind != CallableMemberDescriptor.Kind.FAKE_OVERRIDE\n                && modality != Modality.ABSTRACT\n                && typeParameters.isEmpty()\n                && valueParameters.isEmpty()\n        // Unfortunately, we can't check the return type as it's unresolved in IDE light classes\n    }\n}\n\ninternal fun SimpleFunctionDescriptor.isWriteToParcel(): Boolean {\n    return typeParameters.isEmpty()\n            && valueParameters.size == 2\n            // Unfortunately, we can't check the first parameter type as it's unresolved in IDE light classes\n            && KotlinBuiltIns.isInt(valueParameters[1].type)\n            && returnType?.let { KotlinBuiltIns.isUnit(it) } == true\n}\n\ninterface DESCRIBE_CONTENTS(DESCRIBE_CONTENTS_NAME.identifier),\n        NEW_ARRAY(NEW_ARRAY_NAME.identifier),\n        CREATE_FROM_PARCEL(CREATE_FROM_PARCEL_NAME.identifier)\n    }\n}\n\nfun List<FqName>): Boolean =\n    hasParcelizeAnnotation(parcelizeAnnotations)\n            || getSuperClassNotAny()?.takeIf(DescriptorUtils::isSealedClass)?.hasParcelizeAnnotation(parcelizeAnnotations) == true\n            || getSuperInterfaces().any { DescriptorUtils.isSealedClass(it) && it.hasParcelizeAnnotation(parcelizeAnnotations) }\n\nval KotlinType.isParceler: Boolean\n    get() = constructor.declarationDescriptor?.fqNameSafe == PARCELER_FQN\n\nfun Annotated.findAnyAnnotation(fqNames: List<FqName>): AnnotationDescriptor? {\n    for (fqName in fqNames) {\n        val annotation = annotations.findAnnotation(fqName)\n        if (annotation != null) {\n            return annotation\n        }\n    }\n\n    return null\n}\n\nfun Annotated.hasAnyAnnotation(fqNames: List<FqName>): Boolean {\n    for (fqName in fqNames) {\n        if (annotations.hasAnnotation(fqName)) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n\n    return false\n}\n\nfun getTypeParcelers(annotations: Annotations): List<TypeParcelerMapping> {\n    val serializers = mutableListOf<TypeParcelerMapping>()\n\n    for (annotation in annotations.filter { it.fqName in ParcelizeNames.TYPE_PARCELER_FQ_NAMES }) {\n        val (mappedType, parcelerType) = annotation.type.arguments.takeIf { it.size == 2 } ?: continue\n        serializers += TypeParcelerMapping(mappedType.type, parcelerType.type)\n    }\n\n Complete File Content\n\n```kotlin\n/*\n * Copyright 2010-2018 JetBrains s.r.o. and Kotlin Programming Language contributors.\n * Use of this source code is governed by the Apache 2.0 license that can org.jetbrains.kotlin.diagnostics.DiagnosticSink\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.incremental.components.NoLookupLocation\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.lexer.KtTokens\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.name.FqName\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.parcelize.ParcelizeNames.OLD_PARCELER_FQN\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.parcelize.ParcelizeNames.PARCELABLE_FQN\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.parcelize.diagnostic.ErrorsParcelize\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.parcelize.serializers.isParcelable\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.parcelize.serializers.matchesFqNameWithSupertypes\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.psi.*\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.resolve.BindingContext\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.resolve.checkers.DeclarationChecker\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.resolve.checkers.DeclarationCheckerContext\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.resolve.descriptorUtil.fqNameSafe\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.resolve.descriptorUtil.getSuperClassNotAny\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.resolve.jvm.annotations.findJvmFieldAnnotation\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.types.KotlinType\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.types.TypeUtils\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.types.isError\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.types.typeUtil.representativeUpperBound\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.types.typeUtil.supertypes\n\nopen class ParcelizeDeclarationChecker(\n    val parcelizeAnnotations: List<FqName>,\n    private val experimentalCodeGeneration: Boolean = false,\n) : DeclarationChecker {\n    private companion object {\n        private val IGNORED_ON_PARCEL_FQ_NAMES = listOf(\n            FqName(\"kotlinx.parcelize.IgnoredOnParcel\"),\n            FqName(\"kotlinx.android.parcel.IgnoredOnParcel\")\n        )\n    }\n\n    override fun check(declaration: KtDeclaration, descriptor: DeclarationDescriptor, context: DeclarationCheckerContext) {\n        val trace = context.trace\n\n        when (descriptor) {\n            is ClassDescriptor -> {\n                checkParcelableClass(descriptor, declaration, trace, trace.bindingContext, context.languageVersionSettings)\n                checkParcelerClass(descriptor, declaration, trace)\n            }\n            is SimpleFunctionDescriptor -> {\n                val containingClass = descriptor.containingDeclaration as? ClassDescriptor\n                val ktFunction = declaration as? KtFunction\n                if (containingClass != null && ktFunction != null) {\n                    checkParcelableClassMethod(descriptor, containingClass, ktFunction, trace)\n                }\n            }\n            is PropertyDescriptor -> {\n                val containingClass = descriptor.containingDeclaration as? ClassDescriptor\n                val ktProperty = declaration as? KtProperty\n                if (containingClass != null && ktProperty != null) {\n                    checkParcelableClassProperty(descriptor, containingClass, ktProperty, trace, trace.bindingContext)\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun checkParcelableClassMethod(\n        method: SimpleFunctionDescriptor,\n        containingClass: ClassDescriptor,\n        declaration: KtFunction,\n        diagnosticHolder: DiagnosticSink\n    ) {\n        if (!containingClass.isParcelize(parcelizeAnnotations)) {\n            return\n        }\n\n        if (method.isWriteToParcel() && declaration.hasModifier(KtTokens.OVERRIDE_KEYWORD)) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.modifierList?.getModifier(KtTokens.OVERRIDE_KEYWORD)\n                ?: declaration.nameIdentifier\n                ?: declaration\n\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.OVERRIDING_WRITE_TO_PARCEL_IS_NOT_ALLOWED.on(reportElement))\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun checkParcelableClassProperty(\n        property: PropertyDescriptor,\n        containingClass: ClassDescriptor,\n        declaration: KtProperty,\n        diagnosticHolder: DiagnosticSink,\n        bindingContext: BindingContext\n    ) {\n        fun hasIgnoredOnParcel(): Boolean {\n            fun Annotations.hasIgnoredOnParcel() = any { it.fqName in IGNORED_ON_PARCEL_FQ_NAMES }\n\n            return property.annotations.hasIgnoredOnParcel() || (property.getter?.annotations?.hasIgnoredOnParcel() ?: false)\n        }\n\n        if (containingClass.isParcelize(parcelizeAnnotations)\n            && (declaration.hasDelegate() || bindingContext[BindingContext.BACKING_FIELD_REQUIRED, property] == true)\n            && !hasIgnoredOnParcel()\n            && !containingClass.hasCustomParceler()\n        ) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PROPERTY_WONT_BE_SERIALIZED.on(reportElement))\n        }\n\n        // @JvmName is not applicable to property so we can check just the descriptor name\n        if (property.name.asString() == \"CREATOR\" && property.findJvmFieldAnnotation() != null && containingClass.isCompanionObject) {\n            val outerClass = containingClass.containingDeclaration as? ClassDescriptor\n            if (outerClass != null && outerClass.isParcelize(parcelizeAnnotations)) {\n                val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n                diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.CREATOR_DEFINITION_IS_NOT_ALLOWED.on(reportElement))\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun checkParcelerClass(\n        descriptor: ClassDescriptor,\n        declaration: KtDeclaration,\n        diagnosticHolder: DiagnosticSink,\n    ) {\n        if (!descriptor.isCompanionObject || declaration !is KtObjectDeclaration) {\n            return\n        }\n\n        for (type in descriptor.defaultType.supertypes()) {\n            if (type.constructor.declarationDescriptor?.fqNameSafe == OLD_PARCELER_FQN) {\n                val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration.getObjectKeyword() ?: declaration\n                diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.DEPRECATED_PARCELER.on(reportElement))\n                break\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun checkParcelableClass(\n        descriptor: ClassDescriptor,\n        declaration: KtDeclaration,\n        diagnosticHolder: DiagnosticSink,\n        bindingContext: BindingContext,\n        languageVersionSettings: LanguageVersionSettings\n    ) {\n        if (!descriptor.isParcelize(parcelizeAnnotations)) {\n            return\n        }\n\n        if (declaration !is KtClassOrObject) {\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_SHOULD_BE_CLASS.on(declaration))\n            return\n        }\n\n        if (declaration is KtClass && (declaration.isAnnotation() || declaration.isInterface() && !declaration.isSealed())) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_SHOULD_BE_CLASS.on(reportElement))\n            return\n        }\n\n        for (companion in declaration.companionObjects) {\n            if (companion.name == \"CREATOR\") {\n                val reportElement = companion.nameIdentifier ?: companion\n                diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.CREATOR_DEFINITION_IS_NOT_ALLOWED.on(reportElement))\n            }\n        }\n\n        val abstractModifier = declaration.modifierList?.getModifier(KtTokens.ABSTRACT_KEYWORD)\n        if (abstractModifier != null) {\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_SHOULD_BE_INSTANTIABLE.on(abstractModifier))\n        }\n\n        if (declaration is KtClass && declaration.isInner()) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.modifierList?.getModifier(KtTokens.INNER_KEYWORD) ?: declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_CANT_BE_INNER_CLASS.on(reportElement))\n        }\n\n        if (declaration.isLocal) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_CANT_BE_LOCAL_CLASS.on(reportElement))\n        }\n\n        val superTypes = TypeUtils.getAllSupertypes(descriptor.defaultType)\n        if (superTypes.none { it.constructor.declarationDescriptor?.fqNameSafe == PARCELABLE_FQN }) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.NO_PARCELABLE_SUPERTYPE.on(reportElement))\n        }\n\n        for (supertypeEntry in declaration.superTypeListEntries) {\n            supertypeEntry as? KtDelegatedSuperTypeEntry ?: continue\n            val delegateExpression = supertypeEntry.delegateExpression ?: continue\n            val type = bindingContext[BindingContext.TYPE, supertypeEntry.typeReference] ?: continue\n            if (type.isParcelable()) {\n                val reportElement = supertypeEntry.byKeywordNode?.psi ?: delegateExpression\n                diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_DELEGATE_IS_NOT_ALLOWED.on(reportElement))\n            }\n        }\n\n        // The constructor checks are irrelevant for custom parcelers\n        if (descriptor.hasCustomParceler()) {\n            return\n        }\n        val primaryConstructor = declaration.primaryConstructor\n        if (primaryConstructor == null && declaration.secondaryConstructors.isNotEmpty()) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_SHOULD_HAVE_PRIMARY_CONSTRUCTOR.on(reportElement))\n        } else if (primaryConstructor != null && primaryConstructor.valueParameters.isEmpty()) {\n            val reportElement = declaration.nameIdentifier ?: declaration\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_PRIMARY_CONSTRUCTOR_IS_EMPTY.on(reportElement))\n        }\n\n        for (parameter in primaryConstructor?.valueParameters.orEmpty<KtParameter>()) {\n            checkParcelableClassProperty(parameter, descriptor, declaration.body, diagnosticHolder, bindingContext, languageVersionSettings)\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun checkParcelableClassProperty(\n        parameter: KtParameter,\n        containerClass: ClassDescriptor,\n        containerClassBody: KtClassBody?,\n        diagnosticHolder: DiagnosticSink,\n        bindingContext: BindingContext,\n        languageVersionSettings: LanguageVersionSettings\n    ) {\n        if (!parameter.hasValOrVar()) {\n            if (containerClass.allowBareValueArguments()) {\n                if (containerClassBody != null) {\n                    FindParameterReferences(setOf(parameter), bindingContext, diagnosticHolder).visitElement(containerClassBody)\n                }\n            } else {\n                val reportElement = parameter.nameIdentifier ?: parameter\n                diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_CONSTRUCTOR_PARAMETER_SHOULD_BE_VAL_OR_VAR.on(reportElement))\n            }\n        } else {\n\n            val descriptor = bindingContext[BindingContext.PRIMARY_CONSTRUCTOR_PARAMETER, parameter] ?: return\n\n            // Don't check parameters which won't be serialized\n            if (descriptor.annotations.any { it.fqName in IGNORED_ON_PARCEL_FQ_NAMES }) {\n                return\n            }\n\n            val type = descriptor.type\n            if (!type.isError) {\n                val customParcelerTypes =\n                    (getTypeParcelers(descriptor.annotations) + getTypeParcelers(containerClass.annotations)).map { (mappedType, _) ->\n                        mappedType\n                    }.toSet()\n\n                val unsupported = checkParcelableType(type, customParcelerTypes, containerClass, languageVersionSettings)\n                val reportElement = parameter.typeReference ?: parameter.nameIdentifier ?: parameter\n                if (type in unsupported) {\n                    diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_TYPE_NOT_SUPPORTED.on(reportElement))\n                } else {\n                    unsupported.forEach {\n                        diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.PARCELABLE_TYPE_CONTAINS_NOT_SUPPORTED.on(reportElement, it))\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Returns the set of types that are *not* supported. This set can include types other than `type`\n    // if it is a generally supported container type that contains unsupported elements in this instantiation.\n    private fun checkParcelableType(\n        type: KotlinType,\n        customParcelerTypes: Set<KotlinType>,\n        containerClass: ClassDescriptor,\n        languageVersionSettings: LanguageVersionSettings,\n        inDataClass: Boolean = false,\n    ): Set<KotlinType> {\n        if (type.hasAnyAnnotation(ParcelizeNames.RAW_VALUE_ANNOTATION_FQ_NAMES)\n            || type.hasAnyAnnotation(ParcelizeNames.WRITE_WITH_FQ_NAMES)\n            || type in customParcelerTypes\n            || type.isBuiltinFunctionalTypeOrSubtype\n        ) return emptySet()\n\n        val upperBound = type.getErasedUpperBound()\n        val descriptor = upperBound.constructor.declarationDescriptor as? ClassDescriptor\n            ?: return setOf(type)\n\n        if (descriptor.kind.isSingleton || descriptor.kind.isEnumClass) {\n            return emptySet()\n        }\n\n        val fqName = descriptor.fqNameSafe.asString()\n        if (fqName in BuiltinParcelableTypes.PARCELABLE_BASE_TYPE_FQNAMES) {\n            return emptySet()\n        }\n\n        if (fqName in BuiltinParcelableTypes.PARCELABLE_CONTAINER_FQNAMES) {\n            return upperBound.arguments.fold(emptySet()) { acc, arg ->\n                acc union checkParcelableType(arg.type, customParcelerTypes, containerClass, languageVersionSettings)\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (BuiltinParcelableTypes.PARCELABLE_SUPERTYPE_FQNAMES.any { type.matchesFqNameWithSupertypes(it) }) {\n            return emptySet()\n        }\n\n        if (descriptor.isData && (inDataClass || type.annotations.hasAnnotation(ParcelizeNames.DATA_CLASS_ANNOTATION_FQ_NAME))) {\n            val scope = descriptor.getMemberScope(type.arguments)\n            val primaryConstructor = descriptor.constructors.find { it.isPrimary } ?: return setOf(type)\n            val properties = primaryConstructor.valueParameters.map {\n                scope.getContributedVariables(it.name, NoLookupLocation.FOR_ALREADY_TRACKED).first()\n            }\n            // Serialization uses the property getters, deserialization uses the constructor.\n            if (!DescriptorVisibilityUtils.isVisible(null, primaryConstructor, containerClass, languageVersionSettings) ||\n                properties.any { !DescriptorVisibilityUtils.isVisible(null, it, containerClass, languageVersionSettings) }\n            ) return setOf(type)\n\n            return properties.fold(emptySet()) { acc, property ->\n                acc union checkParcelableType(\n                    property.type, customParcelerTypes, containerClass, languageVersionSettings, inDataClass = true\n                )\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (BuiltinParcelableTypes.EXTERNAL_SERIALIZABLE_FQNAMES.any { type.matchesFqNameWithSupertypes(it) }) {\n            return emptySet()\n        }\n\n        return setOf(type)\n    }\n\n    private fun KotlinType.getErasedUpperBound(): KotlinType =\n        (constructor.declarationDescriptor as? TypeParameterDescriptor)?.representativeUpperBound?.getErasedUpperBound()\n            ?: this\n\n    private fun ClassDescriptor.hasCustomParceler(): Boolean {\n        val companionObjectSuperTypes = companionObjectDescriptor?.let { TypeUtils.getAllSupertypes(it.defaultType) } ?: return false\n        return companionObjectSuperTypes.any { it.isParceler }\n    }\n\n    private fun ClassDescriptor.allowBareValueArguments(): Boolean {\n        val inheritsFromParcelize = isParcelize(parcelizeAnnotations) && (getSuperClassNotAny()?.isParcelize(parcelizeAnnotations) == true)\n        return experimentalCodeGeneration && inheritsFromParcelize && !hasCustomParcelerInChain()\n    }\n\n    private fun ClassDescriptor.hasCustomParcelerInChain(): Boolean =\n        hasCustomParceler() || getSuperClassNotAny()?.hasCustomParcelerInChain() == true\n\n}\n\nclass FindParameterReferences(\n    lookingFor: Set<KtParameter>,\n    private val bindingContext: BindingContext,\n    private val diagnosticHolder: DiagnosticSink,\n) : KtTreeVisitorVoid() {\n\n    private val lookingForDescriptors = lookingFor.map {\n        bindingContext[BindingContext.VALUE_PARAMETER, it]\n    }\n\n    override fun visitReferenceExpression(expression: KtReferenceExpression) {\n        super.visitReferenceExpression(expression)\n        val parameter = bindingContext[BindingContext.REFERENCE_TARGET, expression] as? ValueParameterDescriptor ?: return\n        if (parameter in lookingForDescriptors) {\n            diagnosticHolder.report(ErrorsParcelize.VALUE_PARAMETER_USED_IN_CLASS_BODY.on(expression))\n        }\n    }\n}\n```"}]},"uuid":"d73bec12-51dd-4260-b45c-5574d2ccfc27","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:19:02.768Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"5e456979-0dea-4972-9e1c-d9caa2b3a99c","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

androidSymbols: AndroidSymbols,\n    parcelizeAnnotations: List<FqName>,\n    experimentalCodeGeneration: Boolean,\n) : ParcelizeIrTransformerBase(context, androidSymbols, parcelizeAnnotations, experimentalCodeGeneration) {\n\n    fun transform(moduleFragment: IrModuleFragment) {\n        moduleFragment.accept(this, null)\n        deferredOperations.forEach { it() }\n\n        moduleFragment.transformChildrenVoid(object : IrElementTransformerVoid() {\n            override fun visitCall(expression: IrCall): IrExpression {\n                val callee = expression.symbol.owner\n                if (callee.isParcelableCreatorIntrinsic()) {\n                    expression.typeArguments[0]?.getClass()?.let { parcelableClass ->\n                        androidSymbols.createBuilder(expression.symbol).apply {\n                            return getParcelableCreator(parcelableClass)\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                return expression\n            }\n        })\n    }\n\n    override fun visitElement(element: IrElement) = element.acceptChildren(this, null)\n\n    override fun visitClass(declaration: IrClass) {\n        declaration.acceptChildren(this, null)\n\n        // Sealed classes can be annotated with `@Parcelize`, but that only implies that we\n        // should process their immediate subclasses.\n        if (!declaration.isParcelize(parcelizeAnnotations))\n            return\n\n        val parcelableProperties = declaration.parcelableProperties\n\n        // If the companion extends Parceler, it can override parts of the generated implementation.\n        val parcelerObject = declaration.companionObject()?.takeIf {\n            it.isSubclassOfFqName(PARCELER_FQN.asString())\n        }\n        val generateInheritanceConstructor = declaration.canGenerateInheritanceConstructor()\n        if (generateInheritanceConstructor) {\n            // The signature for this constructor is not generated in [FirParcelizeDeclarationGenerator] so the checks\n            // need to be repeated here. This is on purpose. The declaration generator does not see through `expect` and `actual`\n            // which prevents us from checking if the construct's property has been marked with `IgnoredOnParcel` and should\n            // not be part of this specialized constructor.\n            declaration.addConstructor {}.apply {\n                origin = GeneratedByPlugin(ParcelizePluginKey)\n                val constructorArguments = declaration.inheritanceConstructorArguments()\n                constructorArguments.forEach {\n                    addValueParameter(it.field.name, it.field.type)\n                }\n                addValueParameter(ParcelizeNames.MARKER_NAME, androidSymbols.directInitializerMarker.defaultType)\n                // Might reference constructors from super classes and those might not be yet generated.\n                // This is why defer here is needed. We will have signature but not body.\n                defer {\n                    generateInheritanceConstructor(declaration, parcelableProperties, constructorArguments)\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // At this point we generated constructor for the sealed class and there is nothing more to do.\n        if (declaration.modality == Modality.SEALED)\n            return\n\n        for (function in declaration.functions) {\n            val origin = function.origin\n            if (origin !is GeneratedByPlugin || origin.pluginKey != ParcelizePluginKey) continue\n            when (function.name.identifier) {\n                ParcelizeSyntheticComponent.ComponentKind.DESCRIBE_CONTENTS.methodName -> {\n                    function.generateDescribeContentsBody(parcelableProperties)\n                }\n                ParcelizeSyntheticComponent.ComponentKind.WRITE_TO_PARCEL.methodName -> {\n                    function.apply {\n                        val (receiverParameter, parcelParameter, flagsParameter) = function.parameters\n\n                        // We need to defer the construction of the writer, since it may refer to the [writeToParcel] methods in other\n                        // @Parcelize classes in the current module, which might not be constructed yet at this point.\n                        defer {\n                            if (generateInheritanceConstructor) {\n                                generateWriteToParcelBodyForInheritanceConstructor(\n                                    declaration,\n                                    parcelableProperties,\n                                    receiverParameter,\n                                    parcelParameter,\n                                    flagsParameter\n                                )\n                            } else {\n                                generateWriteToParcelBody(\n                                    declaration,\n                                    parcelerObject,\n                                    parcelableProperties,\n                                    receiverParameter,\n                                    parcelParameter,\n                                    flagsParameter\n                                )\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                else -> error(\"Generated declaration with unknown name: ${function.render()}\")\n            }\n        }\n\n        generateCreator(declaration, parcelerObject, parcelableProperties)\n    }\n}\n```"}]},"uuid":"c00ec659-321d-407f-902f-38cc6f7633ce","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:19:16.802Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"97b43086-d3e5-4276-99b6-f38e02c63f5b","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

Complete File Content\n\n```kotlin\n/*\n * Copyright 2023-2024 JetBrains s.r.o. and Kotlin Programming Language contributors.\n * Use of this source code is governed by the Apache 2.0 license that can kotlinx.collections.immutable.PersistentMap\nimport kotlinx.collections.immutable.persistentListOf\nimport kotlinx.collections.immutable.persistentMapOf\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.backend.common.IrElementTransformerVoidWithContext\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.backend.common.extensions.IrPluginContext\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.ir.expressions.IrCall\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.ir.expressions.IrExpression\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.ir.symbols.IrTypeParameterSymbol\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.name.ClassId\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.name.FqName\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertDiagnostics.POWER_ASSERT_CAPABLE_OVERLOAD_MISSING\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertDiagnostics.POWER_ASSERT_CONSTANT\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertDiagnostics.POWER_ASSERT_FUNCTION_NOT_TRANSFORMED\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertDiagnostics.POWER_ASSERT_RUNTIME_UNAVAILABLE\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertNames.POWER_ASSERT_CLASS_ID\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertNames.POWER_ASSERT_IGNORE_CLASS_ID\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.builder.call.CallBuilder\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.builder.call.LambdaCallBuilder\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.builder.call.SamConversionLambdaCallBuilder\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.builder.call.SimpleCallBuilder\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.builder.parameter.*\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.diagram.*\n\nclass PowerAssertCallTransformer(\n    private val sourceFile: SourceFile,\n    private val context: IrPluginContext,\n    private val configuration: PowerAssertConfiguration,\n    private val builtIns: PowerAssertBuiltIns?,\n    private val factory: PowerAssertFunctionFactory?,\n    private val explanationFactory: ExplanationFactory?\n) : IrElementTransformerVoidWithContext() {\n    private val irTypeSystemContext = IrTypeSystemContextImpl(context.irBuiltIns)\n\n    override fun visitCall(expression: IrCall): IrExpression {\n        expression.transformChildrenVoid()\n\n        val currentFunction = currentFunction?.irElement as? IrSimpleFunction\n        val function = expression.symbol.owner\n        return when {\n            // Never transform recursive calls.\n            expression.symbol == currentFunction?.symbol -> expression\n            // Never transform calls to super instance of the same function. TODO is there a better check for this?\n            expression.superQualifierSymbol != null && expression.symbol in currentFunction?.overriddenSymbols.orEmpty() -> expression\n            // Called function is annotated with @PowerAssert so should be transformed with CallExplanation.\n            function.hasAnnotationOrOverridden(POWER_ASSERT_CLASS_ID) -> buildForAnnotated(expression, function)\n            // Call has no parameters to transform.\n            function.parameters.isEmpty() -> expression\n            // Called function is part of configuration so should be transformed with raw string diagram.\n            function.kotlinFqName in configuration.functions -> buildForOverride(expression, function)\n            // Not a transformable function call.\n            else -> expression\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun buildForAnnotated(\n        originalCall: IrCall,\n        function: IrSimpleFunction,\n    ): IrExpression {\n        if (builtIns == null || explanationFactory == null || factory == null) {\n            // An IrAnnotation is never created for an unknown annotation.\n            // This means this check is entirely pointless as we cannot have an annotated function\n            // if the runtime library is missing.\n            context.diagnosticReporter.at(originalCall, currentFile)\n                .report(POWER_ASSERT_RUNTIME_UNAVAILABLE)\n            return originalCall\n        }\n\n        val synthetic = factory.find(function)\n        if (synthetic == null) {\n            context.diagnosticReporter.at(originalCall, currentFile)\n                .report(POWER_ASSERT_FUNCTION_NOT_TRANSFORMED, function.kotlinFqName)\n            return originalCall\n        }\n\n        val diagramBuilder = CallExplanationParameterBuilder(explanationFactory, sourceFile, originalCall)\n        val callBuilder = LambdaCallBuilder(synthetic, originalCall, builtIns.function0CallExplanationType, builtIns.callExplanationType)\n        val roots = buildArgumentRoots(callBuilder, function, originalCall)\n        return buildPowerAssertCall(originalCall, callBuilder, diagramBuilder, roots)\n    }\n\n    private fun buildForOverride(originalCall: IrCall, function: IrSimpleFunction): IrExpression {\n        // Find a valid delegate function or do not translate\n        // TODO better way to determine which delegate to actually use\n        val callBuilders = findCallBuilders(function, originalCall)\n        val callBuilder = callBuilders.maxByOrNull { builder ->\n            builder.targetFunction.parameters.count { it.kind == IrParameterKind.Regular }\n        }\n\n        if (callBuilder == null) {\n            val regularParameters = function.parameters.filter { it.kind == IrParameterKind.Regular }\n            val valueTypesTruncated = regularParameters.subList(0, regularParameters.size - 1)\n                .joinToString(\"\") { it.type.render() + \", \" }\n            val valueTypesAll = regularParameters.joinToString(\"\") { it.type.render() + \", \" }\n            context.diagnosticReporter.at(originalCall, currentFile)\n                .report(POWER_ASSERT_CAPABLE_OVERLOAD_MISSING, function.kotlinFqName, valueTypesTruncated, valueTypesAll)\n            return super.visitCall(originalCall)\n        }\n\n        val roots = buildArgumentRoots(callBuilder, function, originalCall)\n\n        // If all roots are non-visible, there are no transformable parameters\n        if (roots.all { !it.isVisible() }) {\n            context.diagnosticReporter.at(originalCall, currentFile)\n                .report(POWER_ASSERT_CONSTANT)\n            return super.visitCall(originalCall)\n        }\n\n        val messageArgument = when (callBuilder.targetFunction.parameters.size) {\n            function.parameters.size -> originalCall.arguments.last()\n            else -> null\n        }\n        val parameterBuilder = if (explanationFactory != null) {\n            val diagramBuilder = CallExplanationParameterBuilder(explanationFactory, sourceFile, originalCall)\n            DefaultMessageParameterBuilder(explanationFactory, function, messageArgument, diagramBuilder)\n        } else {\n            StringParameterBuilder(sourceFile, originalCall, function, messageArgument)\n        }\n\n        return buildPowerAssertCall(originalCall, callBuilder, parameterBuilder, roots)\n    }\n\n    private fun buildArgumentRoots(\n        callBuilder: CallBuilder,\n        function: IrSimpleFunction,\n        originalCall: IrCall,\n    ): List<RootNode<IrValueParameter>> {\n        val argumentCount = when (callBuilder.targetFunction.parameters.size) {\n            function.parameters.size -> originalCall.arguments.size - 1\n            else -> originalCall.arguments.size\n        }\n        return (0..<argumentCount).map {\n            val parameter = function.parameters[it]\n            val argument = originalCall.arguments[it]\n\n            // Check if the parameter or parameter type should be ignored.\n            if (\n                parameter.hasAnnotation(POWER_ASSERT_IGNORE_CLASS_ID) ||\n                parameter.type.getClass()?.hasAnnotation(POWER_ASSERT_IGNORE_CLASS_ID) == true\n            ) {\n                val root = RootNode(parameter)\n                if (argument != null) root.addChild(HiddenNode(argument))\n                root\n            } else {\n                buildTree(parameter, argument)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun buildPowerAssertCall(\n        originalCall: IrCall,\n        callBuilder: CallBuilder,\n        parameterBuilder: ParameterBuilder,\n        roots: List<RootNode<IrValueParameter>>\n    ): IrExpression {\n        val symbol = currentScope!!.scope.scopeOwnerSymbol\n        val builder = DeclarationIrBuilder(context, symbol, originalCall.startOffset, originalCall.endOffset)\n\n        fun recursive(\n            index: Int,\n            arguments: PersistentList<IrExpression?>,\n            argumentVariables: PersistentMap<IrValueParameter, List<IrDiagramVariable>>,\n        ): IrExpression {\n            if (index >= roots.size) {\n                val diagram = parameterBuilder.build(builder, argumentVariables)\n                return callBuilder.buildCall(builder, arguments, diagram)\n            } else {\n                val root = roots[index]\n                val child = root.children.singleOrNull()\n                if (child == null) {\n                    val newArguments = arguments.add(originalCall.arguments[index])\n                    return recursive(index + 1, newArguments, argumentVariables)\n                } else {\n                    return builder.buildDiagramNesting(sourceFile, child) { argument, newVariables ->\n                        val newArguments = arguments.add(argument)\n                        val newArgumentVariables = argumentVariables.put(root.parameter, newVariables)\n                        recursive(index + 1, newArguments, newArgumentVariables)\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        return recursive(0, persistentListOf(), persistentMapOf())\n    }\n\n    private fun findCallBuilders(function: IrFunction, original: IrCall): List<CallBuilder> {\n        val values = function.parameters\n        if (values.isEmpty()) return emptyList()\n\n        val finder = context.finderForSource(sourceFile.irFile)\n        // Java static functions require searching by class\n        val parentClassFunctions = (\n                function.parentClassId\n                    ?.let { finder.findClass(it) }\n                    ?.functions ?: emptySequence()\n                )\n            .filter { it.owner.kotlinFqName == function.kotlinFqName }\n            .toList()\n        val possible = (finder.findFunctions(function.callableId) + parentClassFunctions)\n            .distinct()\n\n        return possible.mapNotNull { overload ->\n            // Type parameters must be compatible.\n            if (function.typeParameters.size != overload.owner.typeParameters.size) {\n                return@mapNotNull null\n            }\n            for (i in function.typeParameters.indices) {\n                val functionSuperTypes = function.typeParameters[i].superTypes\n                val overloadDefaultType = overload.owner.typeParameters[i].defaultType\n                if (functionSuperTypes.any { !it.isAssignableTo(overloadDefaultType) }) {\n                    return@mapNotNull null\n                }\n            }\n\n            fun IrType.remap(): IrType = remapTypeParameters(overload.owner, function)\n\n            // Value parameters must be compatible.\n            val parameters = overload.owner.parameters\n            if (parameters.size !in values.size..values.size + 1) return@mapNotNull null\n            for (i in values.indices) {\n                val value = values[i]\n                val parameter = parameters[i]\n                if (value.kind != parameter.kind) return@mapNotNull null\n\n                when (value.kind) {\n                    // Regular parameters may only be assignable.\n                    IrParameterKind.Regular,\n                        -> if (!value.type.isAssignableTo(parameter.type.remap())) return@mapNotNull null\n\n                    // All other parameter kinds must match exactly.\n                    IrParameterKind.DispatchReceiver,\n                    IrParameterKind.Context,\n                    IrParameterKind.ExtensionReceiver,\n                        -> if (value.type != parameter.type.remap()) return@mapNotNull null\n                }\n            }\n\n            val messageParameter = parameters.last()\n            if (messageParameter.kind != IrParameterKind.Regular) return@mapNotNull null\n            val messageType = messageParameter.type\n            return@mapNotNull when {\n                isStringSupertype(messageType) -> SimpleCallBuilder(overload, original)\n                isStringFunction(messageType) -> LambdaCallBuilder(overload, original, messageType, context.irBuiltIns.stringType)\n                isStringJavaSupplierFunction(messageType) -> SamConversionLambdaCallBuilder(overload, original, messageType)\n                else -> null\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun isStringFunction(type: IrType): Boolean =\n        type.isFunctionOrKFunction() && type is IrSimpleType && (type.arguments.size == 1 && isStringSupertype(type.arguments.first()))\n\n    private fun isStringJavaSupplierFunction(type: IrType): Boolean {\n        val javaSupplier = context.finderForBuiltins().findClass(ClassId.topLevel(FqName(\"java.util.function.Supplier\")))\n        return javaSupplier != null && type.isSubtypeOfClass(javaSupplier) &&\n                type is IrSimpleType && (type.arguments.size == 1 && isStringSupertype(type.arguments.first()))\n    }\n\n    private fun isStringSupertype(argument: IrTypeArgument): Boolean =\n        argument is IrTypeProjection && isStringSupertype(argument.type)\n\n    private fun isStringSupertype(type: IrType): Boolean =\n        context.irBuiltIns.stringType.isSubtypeOf(type, irTypeSystemContext)\n\n    private fun IrType?.isAssignableTo(type: IrType?): Boolean {\n        if (this != null && type != null) {\n            if (isSubtypeOf(type, irTypeSystemContext)) return true\n            val superTypes = (type.classifierOrNull as? IrTypeParameterSymbol)?.owner?.superTypes\n            return superTypes != null && superTypes.all { isSubtypeOf(it, irTypeSystemContext) }\n        } else {\n            return this == null && type == null\n        }\n    }\n}\n```"}]},"uuid":"552cfbb5-ff37-40f0-934a-2e55268e6cf1","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:19:37.597Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"ebf5aebc-629f-49dc-a790-27ce0e55c105","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

File Content\n\nThis is a Kotlin source file from the JetBrains Kotlin project (2010-2016) licensed under Apache License 2.0.\n\n## Overview\n\nThe file defines `KaptCommandLineProcessor`, which implements the `CommandLineProcessor` interface for handling Kotlin annotation processing tool (KAPT) command-line options.\n\n## Key Components\n\n**Main Class**: Processes compiler plugin options related to annotation processing, including:\n\n- Output directories (sources, classes, stubs, incremental data)\n- File tracking (changed files, compiled sources, incremental cache)\n- Annotation processor configuration (classpath, processor names)\n- Processing options and javac settings\n- Various feature flags (verbose mode, light analysis, strict mode, etc.)\n\n**Helper Functions**:\n- `setFlag()` - Toggles boolean flags\n- `setSelector()` - Assigns enum-based configuration values\n- `setKeyValue()` - Parses and applies key=value pairs\n- `decodeMap()` - Deserializes Base64-encoded option maps using Java serialization\n\n**Special Handling**: The code includes deprecated option support and delegates certain options like `CONFIGURATION` to be handled elsewhere in the compilation pipeline.\n\nThe implementation validates input values and throws `CliOptionProcessingException` for invalid configurations."}]},"uuid":"6f572a25-f2ca-4a1c-9a3b-c1c5700bcb4d","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:19:51.044Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"a435f250-e92d-45a3-9b96-6c838350d352","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

Here's the complete file content as requested:\n\n```kotlin\n/*\n * Copyright 2010-2025 JetBrains s.r.o. and Kotlin Programming Language contributors.\n * Use of this source code is governed by the Apache 2.0 license that can be found in the license/LICENSE.txt file.\n */\n\npackage org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt\n\nimport com.intellij.openapi.Disposable\nimport com.intellij.openapi.project.Project\nimport com.intellij.openapi.util.Disposer\nimport com.sun.tools.javac.tree.JCTree\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.common.*\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.common.fir.FirDiagnosticsCompilerResultsReporter\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.common.messages.CompilerMessageSeverity.OUTPUT\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.common.messages.MessageCollector\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.common.messages.OutputMessageUtil\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.common.modules.ModuleChunk\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.common.output.writeAll\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.jvm.compiler.KotlinToJVMBytecodeCompiler\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.jvm.config.JavaSourceRoot\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.jvm.config.JvmClasspathRoot\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.pipeline.ConfigurationPipelineArtifact\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.pipeline.PipelineArtifact\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.pipeline.jvm.JvmBackendPipelinePhase\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.pipeline.jvm.JvmFir2IrPipelinePhase\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.pipeline.jvm.JvmFrontendPipelineArtifact\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.pipeline.jvm.JvmFrontendPipelinePhase\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.cli.registerExtensionStorage\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.codegen.ClassBuilderMode\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.codegen.OriginCollectingClassBuilderFactory\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.config.*\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.diagnostics.impl.DiagnosticsCollectorImpl\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.builder.FirSyntaxErrors\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.extensions.FirAnalysisHandlerExtension\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.base.*\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.base.util.KaptBaseError\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.base.util.KaptLogger\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.base.util.getPackageNameJava9Aware\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.base.util.info\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.stubs.KaptStubConverter\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.stubs.KaptStubConverter.KaptStub\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.util.MessageCollectorBackedKaptLogger\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt.util.prettyPrint\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.kapt3.diagnostic.KaptError\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.util.PhaseType\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.utils.kapt.MemoryLeakDetector\nimport java.io.File\n\n/**\n * This extension implements K2 kapt by invoking the compiler in the \"skip bodies\" / suppress-errors mode, and translating the resulting\n * in-memory class files to Java sources, correcting error types.\n */\n@OptIn(LegacyK2CliPipeline::class)\nopen class FirKaptAnalysisHandlerExtension(\n    private val kaptLogger: MessageCollectorBackedKaptLogger? = null,\n) : FirAnalysisHandlerExtension() {\n    lateinit var logger: MessageCollectorBackedKaptLogger\n    lateinit var options: KaptOptions\n\n    override fun isApplicable(configuration: CompilerConfiguration): Boolean {\n        return configuration[KAPT_OPTIONS] != null && !configuration.skipBodies\n    }\n\n    override fun doAnalysis(project: Project, configuration: CompilerConfiguration): Boolean {\n        val optionsBuilder = configuration[KAPT_OPTIONS]!!\n        logger = kaptLogger\n            ?: MessageCollectorBackedKaptLogger(\n                KaptFlag.VERBOSE in optionsBuilder.flags,\n                KaptFlag.INFO_AS_WARNINGS in optionsBuilder.flags,\n                configuration.messageCollector,\n            )\n        val messageCollector = logger.messageCollector\n\n        if (optionsBuilder.mode == AptMode.WITH_COMPILATION) {\n            logger.error(\"KAPT \\\"compile\\\" mode is not supported in Kotlin 2.x. Run kapt with -Kapt-mode=stubsAndApt and use kotlinc for the final compilation step.\")\n            return false\n        }\n\n        optionsBuilder.apply {\n            projectBaseDir = projectBaseDir ?: project.basePath?.let(::File)\n            val contentRoots = configuration.contentRoots\n            compileClasspath.addAll(contentRoots.filterIsInstance<JvmClasspathRoot>().map { it.file })\n            javaSourceRoots.addAll(contentRoots.filterIsInstance<JavaSourceRoot>().map { it.file })\n            classesOutputDir = classesOutputDir ?: configuration.outputDirectory\n        }\n\n        optionsBuilder.checkOptions(logger, configuration)?.let { return it }\n\n        options = optionsBuilder.build()\n        if (options[KaptFlag.VERBOSE]) {\n            logger.info(options.logString())\n        }\n\n        if (options.mode.generateStubs) {\n            val updatedConfiguration = configuration.copy().apply {\n                this.messageCollector = messageCollector\n                skipBodies = true\n                useLightTree = false\n\n                /*\n                 * Later the KAPT pipeline registers extensions once again, so the extensions storage\n                 * should be reset. Otherwise the extensions would be duplicated.\n                 */\n                @OptIn(CompilerConfiguration.Internals::class)\n                registerExtensionStorage()\n            }\n            val disposable = Disposer.newDisposable(\"K2KaptSession.project\")\n            try {\n                contextForStubGeneration(disposable, updatedConfiguration)?.use(::generateKotlinSourceStubs)\n            } finally {\n                disposeRootInWriteAction(disposable)\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (!options.mode.runAnnotationProcessing) return true\n\n        createProcessorLoader().use { processorLoader ->\n            val processors = processorLoader.loadProcessors()\n            if (processors.processors.isEmpty()) return true\n\n            val kaptContext = KaptContext(options, false, logger)\n\n            fun handleKaptError(error: KaptError): Boolean {\n                val cause = error.cause\n\n                if (cause != null) {\n                    kaptContext.logger.exception(cause)\n                }\n\n                return false\n            }\n\n            try {\n                runAnnotationProcessing(kaptContext, processors)\n            } catch (error: KaptBaseError) {\n                val kind = when (error.kind) {\n                    KaptBaseError.Kind.EXCEPTION -> KaptError.Kind.EXCEPTION\n                    KaptBaseError.Kind.ERROR_RAISED -> KaptError.Kind.ERROR_RAISED\n                }\n\n                val cause = error.cause\n                return handleKaptError(if (cause != null) KaptError(kind, cause) else KaptError(kind))\n            } catch (error: KaptError) {\n                return handleKaptError(error)\n            } catch (thr: Throwable) {\n                kaptContext.logger.exception(thr)\n                return false\n            } finally {\n                kaptContext.close()\n            }\n        }\n\n        return true\n    }\n\n    private fun runAnnotationProcessing(kaptContext: KaptContext, processors: LoadedProcessors) {\n        if (!options.mode.runAnnotationProcessing) return\n\n        val javaSourceFiles = options.collectJavaSourceFiles(kaptContext.sourcesToReprocess)\n        logger.info { \"Java source files: \" + javaSourceFiles.joinToString { it.normalize().absolutePath } }\n\n        val (annotationProcessingTime) = measureTimeMillis {\n            kaptContext.doAnnotationProcessing(javaSourceFiles, processors.processors)\n        }\n\n        logger.info { \"Annotation processing took $annotationProcessingTime ms\" }\n\n        if (options.detectMemoryLeaks != DetectMemoryLeaksMode.NONE) {\n            MemoryLeakDetector.add(processors.classLoader)\n\n            val isParanoid = options.detectMemoryLeaks == DetectMemoryLeaksMode.PARANOID\n            val (leakDetectionTime, leaks) = measureTimeMillis { MemoryLeakDetector.process(isParanoid) }\n            logger.info { \"Leak detection took $leakDetectionTime ms\" }\n\n            for (leak in leaks) {\n                logger.warn(buildString {\n                    appendLine(\"Memory leak detected!\")\n                    appendLine(\"Location: '${leak.className}', static field '${leak.fieldName}'\")\n                    append(leak.description)\n                })\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    protected open fun updateConfiguration(configuration: CompilerConfiguration) {\n    }\n\n    @OptIn(PipelineArtifact.CliPipelineInternals::class)\n    private fun contextForStubGeneration(disposable: Disposable, configuration: CompilerConfiguration): KaptContextForStubGeneration? {\n        updateConfiguration(configuration)\n        configuration.moduleChunk = ModuleChunk(configuration.modules)\n\n        // We want to ignore all diagnostics except syntax one, which will be checked manually.\n        // So we need to create a new configuration with a separate diagnostics collector, to avoid\n        // reporting any errors into the diagnostics collector of the root configuration, which would be\n        // checked by the main CLI pipeline upon finishing the KAPT stage.\n        val configurationForFrontend = configuration.copy().apply {\n            diagnosticsCollector = DiagnosticsCollectorImpl()\n        }\n\n        val frontendInput = ConfigurationPipelineArtifact(configurationForFrontend, disposable)\n        val frontendOutput = JvmFrontendPipelinePhase.executePhase(frontendInput) ?: return null\n\n        if (checkForSyntaxErrorsAndReport(frontendOutput)) return null\n\n        configuration.perfManager?.notifyPhaseFinished(PhaseType.Analysis)\n\n        // FIR2IR checks for diagnostics in the collector after the main transformation and before const and plugin transformation,\n        // and early returns if there are any errors, so we need to create an empty diagnostics collector once again\n        val configurationForFir2Ir = configuration.copy().apply {\n            diagnosticsCollector = DiagnosticsCollectorImpl()\n        }\n        val fir2IrOutput = JvmFir2IrPipelinePhase.executePhase(\n            frontendOutput.withCompilerConfiguration(configurationForFir2Ir),\n            irGenerationExtensions = emptyList()\n        ) ?: return null\n\n        val builderFactory = OriginCollectingClassBuilderFactory(ClassBuilderMode.KAPT3)\n\n        // JVM backend checks for diagnostics in the collector and early returns if there are any errors\n        // so we need to create an empty diagnostics collector once again\n        val configurationForBackend = configuration.copy().apply {\n            diagnosticsCollector = DiagnosticsCollectorImpl()\n            put(KotlinToJVMBytecodeCompiler.customClassBuilderFactory, builderFactory)\n        }\n        val backendOutput = JvmBackendPipelinePhase.executePhase(fir2IrOutput.withCompilerConfiguration(configurationForBackend))\n        val generationState = backendOutput.outputs.singleOrNull() ?: return null\n\n        return KaptContextForStubGeneration(\n            options, false, logger, builderFactory.compiledClasses, builderFactory.origins, generationState,\n            frontendOutput.frontendOutput.outputs.flatMap { it.fir },\n        )\n    }\n\n    private fun checkForSyntaxErrorsAndReport(frontendOutput: JvmFrontendPipelineArtifact): Boolean {\n        var reported = false\n        FirDiagnosticsCompilerResultsReporter.reportByFile(frontendOutput.configuration.diagnosticsCollector) { diagnostic, location ->\n            if (diagnostic.factory == FirSyntaxErrors.SYNTAX) {\n                FirDiagnosticsCompilerResultsReporter.reportDiagnosticToMessageCollector(\n                    diagnostic,\n                    location,\n                    logger.messageCollector,\n                    frontendOutput.configuration.renderDiagnosticInternalName\n                )\n                reported = true\n            }\n        }\n        return reported\n    }\n\n    private fun generateKotlinSourceStubs(kaptContext: KaptContextForStubGeneration) {\n        val converter = KaptStubConverter(kaptContext, generateNonExistentClass = true)\n\n        val (stubGenerationTime, kaptStubs) = measureTimeMillis {\n            converter.convert()\n        }\n\n        logger.info { \"Java stub generation took $stubGenerationTime ms\" }\n        logger.info { \"Stubs for Kotlin classes: \" + kaptStubs.joinToString { it.file.sourcefile.name } }\n\n        saveStubs(kaptContext, kaptStubs, logger.messageCollector)\n        saveIncrementalData(kaptContext, logger.messageCollector, converter)\n    }\n\n    protected open fun saveStubs(\n        kaptContext: KaptContextForStubGeneration,\n        stubs: List<KaptStub>,\n        messageCollector: MessageCollector,\n    ) {\n        val reportOutputFiles = kaptContext.generationState.configuration.reportOutputFiles\n        val outputFiles = if (reportOutputFiles) kaptContext.generationState.factory.asList().associateBy {\n            it.relativePath.substringBeforeLast(\".class\", missingDelimiterValue = \"\")\n        } else null\n\n        val sourceFiles = mutableListOf<String>()\n\n        for (kaptStub in stubs) {\n            val stub = kaptStub.file\n            val className = (stub.defs.first { it is JCTree.JCClassDecl } as JCTree.JCClassDecl).simpleName.toString()\n\n            val packageName = stub.getPackageNameJava9Aware()?.toString() ?: \"\"\n            val packageDir =\n                if (packageName.isEmpty()) options.stubsOutputDir else File(options.stubsOutputDir, packageName.replace('.', '/'))\n            packageDir.mkdirs()\n\n            val sourceFile = File(packageDir, \"$className.java\")\n            val classFilePathWithoutExtension = if (packageName.isEmpty()) {\n                className\n            } else {\n                \"${packageName.replace('.', '/')}/$className\"\n            }\n\n            sourceFiles += classFilePathWithoutExtension\n\n            fun reportStubsOutputForIC(generatedFile: File) {\n                if (!reportOutputFiles) return\n                if (classFilePathWithoutExtension == \"error/NonExistentClass\") return\n                val sourceFiles = (outputFiles?.get(classFilePathWithoutExtension)\n                    ?: error(\"The `outputFiles` map is not properly initialized (key = $classFilePathWithoutExtension)\")).sourceFiles\n                kaptContext.generationState.configuration.fileMappingTracker?.recordSourceFilesToOutputFileMapping(\n                    sourceFiles,\n                    generatedFile\n                )\n                messageCollector.report(OUTPUT, OutputMessageUtil.formatOutputMessage(sourceFiles, generatedFile))\n            }\n\n            reportStubsOutputForIC(sourceFile)\n            sourceFile.writeText(stub.prettyPrint(kaptContext.context))\n\n            kaptStub.writeMetadataIfNeeded(forSource = sourceFile, ::reportStubsOutputForIC)\n        }\n\n        logger.info { \"Source files: ${sourceFiles}\" }\n    }\n\n    protected open fun saveIncrementalData(\n        kaptContext: KaptContextForStubGeneration,\n        messageCollector: MessageCollector,\n        converter: KaptStubConverter,\n    ) {\n        val incrementalDataOutputDir = options.incrementalDataOutputDir ?: return\n\n        val reportOutputFiles = kaptContext.generationState.configuration.reportOutputFiles\n        kaptContext.generationState.factory.writeAll(incrementalDataOutputDir) { outputInfo, output ->\n            kaptContext.generationState.configuration.fileMappingTracker?.let {\n                when (outputInfo.generatedForCompilerPlugin) {\n                    false -> it.recordSourceFilesToOutputFileMapping(\n                        outputInfo.sourceFiles,\n                        output\n                    )\n\n                    true -> it.recordOutputFileGeneratedForPlugin(output)\n                }\n            }\n            if (reportOutputFiles) {\n                messageCollector.report(OUTPUT, OutputMessageUtil.formatOutputMessage(outputInfo.sourceFiles, output))\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    protected open fun createProcessorLoader(): ProcessorLoader =\n        EfficientProcessorLoader(options, logger)\n\n    private fun KaptOptions.Builder.checkOptions(logger: KaptLogger, configuration: CompilerConfiguration): Boolean? {\n        if (classesOutputDir == null && configuration.outputJar != null) {\n            logger.error(\"Kapt does not support specifying JAR file outputs. Please specify the classes output directory explicitly.\")\n            return false\n        }\n\n        if (processingClasspath.isEmpty()) {\n            // Skip annotation processing if no annotation processors were provided\n            logger.info(\"No annotation processors provided. Skip KAPT processing.\")\n            return true\n        }\n\n        if (sourcesOutputDir == null || classesOutputDir == null || stubsOutputDir == null) {\n            val nonExistentOptionName = when {\n                sourcesOutputDir == null -> \"Sources output directory\"\n                classesOutputDir == null -> \"Classes output directory\"\n                else -> \"Stubs output directory\"\n            }\n            val moduleName = configuration.moduleName ?: configuration.modules.joinToString()\n            logger.warn(\"$nonExistentOptionName is not specified for $moduleName, skipping annotation processing\")\n            return false\n        }\n\n        if (!Kapt.checkJavacComponentsAccess(logger)) {\n            return false\n        }\n\n        return null\n    }\n\n    private inline fun <T> measureTimeMillis(block: () -> T): Pair<Long, T> {\n        val start = System.currentTimeMillis()\n        val result = block()\n        return Pair(System.currentTimeMillis() - start, result)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Key Summary:**\n\nThis extension orchestrates Kotlin 2.x's annotation processing pipeline by converting Kotlin source code into Java stubs, then running annotation processors. The architecture separates concerns: frontend analysis generates FIR (functional intermediate representation), converts to IR (intermediate representation), and backend generates bytecode. The implementation then transforms compiled classes to Java sources, enabling Java-based annotation processors to function with Kotlin 2.x code."}]},"uuid":"f2c8ef95-6482-4c75-9f1f-28739e99f8b2","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:20:20.985Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"e3d3e10c-4a8b-46cc-b246-d7b8c588c81b","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

Here's what it contains:\n\n## Purpose\nThe `PowerAssertFunctionTransformer` class implements a declaration transformer that processes functions annotated with `@PowerAssert`. It's part of Kotlin's power assertion mechanism, which provides enhanced assertion messages.\n\n## Key Components\n\n**Main Class**: Extends `DeclarationTransformer` and takes two parameters:\n- `builtIns`: PowerAssertBuiltIns reference\n- `factory`: PowerAssertFunctionFactory for generating new functions\n\n**Core Method - `transformFlat()`**: \nChecks if a declaration is a simple function with the PowerAssert annotation. If so, it processes the function through the lowering mechanism.\n\n**Lowering Logic**:\nThe `lower()` function performs two actions:\n1. Generates a new power assertion function using the factory\n2. Transforms the original function by replacing `PowerAssert.explanation` references with `null` values\n\nThis dual approach maintains compatibility while ensuring the compiler plugin applies correctly to annotated functions.\n\n## License\nLicensed under Apache 2.0, copyright JetBrains and Kotlin contributors (2010-2024)."}]},"uuid":"8bcb03e6-5fa4-46b1-a1a2-0d97cebc1e00","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:21:28.333Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"48001e9f-8d80-4169-9285-a7bcbc0feb05","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

by irAttribute(copyByDefault = false)\n\nclass PowerAssertFunctionFactory(\n    private val context: IrPluginContext,\n    private val builtIns: PowerAssertBuiltIns,\n) {\n    private val memorizedClassMetadata = hashSetOf<IrClass>()\n\n    fun find(function: IrSimpleFunction): IrSimpleFunctionSymbol? {\n        // If there is an explained symbol:\n        // 1. Function was transformed to generate an explained overload.\n        // 2. Explained overload was already found and saved for faster lookup.\n        function.powerAssertDispatchSymbol?.let { return it }\n\n        // Metadata indicates the function was transformed but is not in the current compilation unit.\n        // If there is no metadata, the function was never compiled with power-assert.\n        val parentClass = function.parent as? IrClass\n        getPowerAssertMetadata(parentClass ?: function) ?: return null\n\n        // Generate a stub-function so a symbol exists which can be called.\n        return generate(function).symbol\n    }\n\n    fun generate(originalFunction: IrSimpleFunction): IrSimpleFunction {\n        originalFunction.powerAssertDispatchSymbol?.let { return it.owner }\n\n        val powerAssertFunction = originalFunction.deepCopyWithSymbols(originalFunction.parent)\n        powerAssertFunction.apply {\n            origin = FUNCTION_FOR_POWER_ASSERT\n            name = Name.identifier(\"${originalFunction.name.identifier}\\$powerassert\")\n            annotations = annotations.filter { !it.isAnnotation(POWER_ASSERT_FQ_NAME) }\n            annotations += createJvmSyntheticAnnotation()\n            val explanationParameter = addValueParameter {\n                name = Name.identifier(\"\\$explanation\")\n                type = builtIns.function0CallExplanationType\n            }\n\n            overriddenSymbols = originalFunction.overriddenSymbols.map { generate(it.owner).symbol }\n\n            // Transform the generated function to use the `$explanation` parameter instead of CallExplain.explanation.\n            transformChildrenVoid(PowerAssertGetExplanationTransformer(builtIns, explanationParameter))\n            // Transform the generated function to propagate the `$explanation` parameter during recursive or super-calls.\n            transformChildrenVoid(PowerAssertSelfCallTransformer(originalFunction, powerAssertFunction, explanationParameter))\n        }\n\n        // Save the power-assert function to the original function to make overload lookup easier.\n        originalFunction.powerAssertDispatchSymbol = powerAssertFunction.symbol\n\n        // Write custom metadata to indicate the original function was indeed compiled with the plugin.\n        // This allows callers to be confident the power-assert function exists, even when calling from a different compilation unit.\n        val parentClass = originalFunction.parent as? IrClass\n        when {\n            parentClass == null -> addPowerAssertMetadata(originalFunction)\n            memorizedClassMetadata.add(parentClass) -> addPowerAssertMetadata(parentClass)\n        }\n\n        return powerAssertFunction\n    }\n\n    private fun createJvmSyntheticAnnotation(): IrAnnotation {\n        val symbol = builtIns.jvmSyntheticAnnotation\n        return IrAnnotationImpl.fromSymbolOwner(\n            startOffset = SYNTHETIC_OFFSET,\n            endOffset = SYNTHETIC_OFFSET,\n            type = symbol.owner.parentAsClass.defaultType,\n            constructorSymbol = symbol,\n        )\n    }\n\n    private fun <E> addPowerAssertMetadata(declaration: E)\n            where E : IrDeclaration, E : IrMetadataSourceOwner {\n        if (declaration.metadata != null) {\n            context.metadataDeclarationRegistrar\n                .addCustomMetadataExtension(declaration, PowerAssertBuiltIns.PLUGIN_ID, builtIns.metadata.data)\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun <E> getPowerAssertMetadata(declaration: E): ByteArray?\n            where E : IrDeclaration, E : IrMetadataSourceOwner {\n        return context.metadataDeclarationRegistrar.getCustomMetadataExtension(declaration, PowerAssertBuiltIns.PLUGIN_ID)\n    }\n}\n```"}]},"uuid":"5237fb71-3de6-4cad-b6ef-4028c50c1e99","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:21:33.613Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"a16d947a-92a6-4155-a9e0-8bf3c06379e5","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

File Content\n\nThis is a Kotlin compiler plugin extension that automatically generates synthetic factory and copy methods for external interfaces annotated with `@JsPlainObjects`.\n\n## Key Components\n\n**Purpose**: The extension generates two synthetic functions in companion objects:\n- An `invoke` operator (factory function) for creating instances\n- A `copy` function for creating modified copies\n\n**Main Class**: `JsPlainObjectsFunctionsGenerator` extends `FirDeclarationGenerationExtension`\n\n**Core Functionality**:\n- Identifies interfaces marked with `@JsPlainObjects` through predicate-based detection\n- Generates companion objects if they don't exist\n- Creates inline functions annotated with `@JsNoDispatchReceiver`\n- Handles type parameters and nullable properties with `VOID` default values\n- Applies `@JsName` annotations for JS property name mapping\n\n**Generated Pattern Example**: For properties in an interface, the factory generates parameters with default values, and the copy function accepts a source parameter plus override fields.\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `generateNestedClassLikeDeclaration()`: Creates companion objects\n- `generateFunctions()`: Produces factory and copy functions\n- `createJsPlainObjectsFunction()`: Core builder for both function types\n\nThe code uses FIR (Frontend Intermediate Representation) APIs for Kotlin compilation and integrates with the JS standard library for proper annotations."}]},"uuid":"c39ea4c1-b6fe-4b50-9caa-e3c9dac7987b","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:21:44.659Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"af18ba25-7d15-44c8-b13c-bcb46167b88b","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

Here's the complete content:\n\n```kotlin\n/*\n * Copyright 2010-2026 JetBrains s.r.o. and Kotlin Programming Language contributors.\n * Use of this source code is governed by the Apache 2.0 license that can be found in the license/LICENSE.txt file.\n */\n\npackage org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.checkers\n\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.diagnostics.DiagnosticReporter\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.diagnostics.reportOn\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.analysis.checkers.MppCheckerKind\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.analysis.checkers.context.CheckerContext\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.analysis.checkers.expression.FirPropertyAccessExpressionChecker\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.expressions.FirPropertyAccessExpression\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.expressions.toResolvedCallableSymbol\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertDiagnostics\nimport org.jetbrains.kotlin.powerassert.PowerAssertNames.POWER_ASSERT_EXPLANATION_CALLABLE_ID\n\ninternal object PowerAssertExplanationAccessChecker : FirPropertyAccessExpressionChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common) {\n    context(context: CheckerContext, reporter: DiagnosticReporter)\n    override fun check(expression: FirPropertyAccessExpression) {\n        // Only check calls to 'PowerAssert.explanation'.\n        if (expression.toResolvedCallableSymbol()?.callableId != POWER_ASSERT_EXPLANATION_CALLABLE_ID) return\n\n        // One of the containers is annotated with '@PowerAssert'.\n        if (context.containingDeclarations.none { it.isPowerAssertFunction() }) {\n            reporter.reportOn(\n                expression.source,\n                PowerAssertDiagnostics.POWER_ASSERT_ILLEGAL_EXPLANATION_ACCESS,\n            )\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Summary:** This checker validates that \"PowerAssert.explanation\" property access occurs only within functions annotated with `@PowerAssert`.
